    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer2638650412703695418">In the Company of Shadows series description:<br/><br/>Years after the bombs of WWIII have changed the physical and political landscape, the Agency ruthlessly works behind the scenes to take down rebel groups that threaten the current government. Their goals justify all means. Hsin Liu Vega (Sin) is their most efficient and deadly assassin ever. However, he tends to go off on unauth</span>
  <span id="freeText2638650412703695418" style="display:none">In the Company of Shadows series description:<br /><br />Years after the bombs of WWIII have changed the physical and political landscape, the Agency ruthlessly works behind the scenes to take down rebel groups that threaten the current government. Their goals justify all means. Hsin Liu Vega (Sin) is their most efficient and deadly assassin ever. However, he tends to go off on unauthorized killing sprees and somehow his assigned partners all end up dead under suspicious circumstances. That is why the Agency has had him locked up in a box on the fourth floor for years. But now they think it is time to put the psychopath back in the field. With a new partner.<br /><br />Boyd's mother, a high ranking Agency official, volunteers her teenage son for the position. Boyd is not afraid of death. In fact, his life has been such an endless cycle of apathy and despair for the last few years that he'd welcome it.<br /><br />Can these two broken men form an efficient partnership? Can they learn to trust anyone, let alone each other? Sin doesn't give a fuck about the Agency, or the androgynous boy who holds the remote to the shock collar that is supposed to control him.<br /><br />On the other hand, Boyd is strangely unafraid of the man everyone calls 'monster' and Sin seems reluctant to let his keeper get himself killed on any missions. Yet.<br />__________<br /><b>Status:</b> Complete<br /><b>Word Count:</b> 404,241 (42 Chapters + Epilogue)</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer496459784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3331704241694578221"><br/><a href='http://s1354.beta.photobucket.com/user/syleegurl13/media/ICoS/0cb2ef8b-33e0-42d2-b34a-7c9c93ceae31_zpsce3d55ab.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403693i/785423.jpg' alt=' photo 0cb2ef8b-33e0-42d2-b34a-7c9c93ceae31_zpsce3d55ab.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <u>AMENDED & FINAL REVIEW:</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Additional thoughts Ch 37 - 42 + epilogue (March 2, 2013)</i>
</b><br/><br/>Good LORD! That is some FANTASTICALLY BRILLIANT stuff!!!!! <br/><br/>"How can they possibly wrap everything up?" "How will it end?" "What happens to...?" GAHHHHH!!!!! The last few chapters were so, so, so GOOD! I can't even...I just...I...I...GAHHHHH!!!! For fans new and old to this series, Sonny & Ais did SO RIGHT by us in how they wrapped this all up. <br/><br/>"Fade" is the BEST book of the series, and "In the Company of </span>
  <span id="freeText3331704241694578221" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://s1354.beta.photobucket.com/user/syleegurl13/media/ICoS/0cb2ef8b-33e0-42d2-b34a-7c9c93ceae31_zpsce3d55ab.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403693i/785423.jpg" alt=" photo 0cb2ef8b-33e0-42d2-b34a-7c9c93ceae31_zpsce3d55ab.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <u>AMENDED &amp; FINAL REVIEW:</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Additional thoughts Ch 37 - 42 + epilogue (March 2, 2013)</i>
</b><br><br>Good LORD! That is some FANTASTICALLY BRILLIANT stuff!!!!! <br><br>"How can they possibly wrap everything up?" "How will it end?" "What happens to...?" GAHHHHH!!!!! The last few chapters were so, so, so GOOD! I can't even...I just...I...I...GAHHHHH!!!! For fans new and old to this series, Sonny &amp; Ais did SO RIGHT by us in how they wrapped this all up. <br><br>"Fade" is the BEST book of the series, and "In the Company of Shadows" is the BEST series I've read...ever...yup...gauntlet thrown...<br><br><u>At the end of it all:</u><br><br><u>Hsin &amp; Boyd</u> - best to you...wherever you end up, whatever you decide (love you, Hsin, forever and ever and ever)<br><u>Kassian &amp; Ryan</u> - stay out of trouble! (Kassian, take care of him!)<br><u>Emilio &amp; Zach</u> - I know, I just know...it's all ok.<br><u>Luke Gerant &amp; Archer</u> - my 2 under-recognized but newly-adored heroes! Welcome to my "favorites" list!<br><br>****************************<br><br><b>
  <i>WIP, review for up to Ch 36 of 42 (January 7, 2013)</i>
</b><br><br>And so it goes…<br><br>Fade, the Final Frontier. Seriously…how do writers come UP with this stuff?! Good lord…this book…<br><br>Ok, if it were a stand-alone, I would say Fade is phenomenal. My only beef w/ Fade as part of the series is that so much of it had our MC’s apart…and at some parts not even really around….so it was hard…I so longed for the other half. <br><br>But, of course Sonny &amp; Ais don’t know how to do anything half-assed. Fade has the <b>TORTURE</b> that you’ve come to sickly crave throughout this series. It also has the <b>LOVE</b> that you’ve come to root for through all the various couples in this series. It has some of the <b>HOTTEST</b> scenes I’ve ever read. And, more so than even in the other books…it had the <b>BEST</b> storyline…ridiculously good…so, so freaking good.<br><br>I can’t express how much Hsin &amp; Boyd, Ryan, Kassian, Emilio, Zach…and all the others, have gotten under my skin and into my heart. Watching them start from angry beginnings, go through near-unbearable anguish, mess-up, make-up, have their lives screwed-up by TPTB, grow-up, and find love along the way…just…no words…<br><br><u>By the end of Ch 36 :</u><br><br><u>Boyd</u> – Beloved …You’ve come a long, long way kid. And though you’ve messed up in the past, as Aiko put it “you make up for it so hard”. Truth.<br><u>Hsin</u> – I don’t want your story to end…You’ve affected me moreso than pretty much any character in a long time. I heart you. Be happy…<br><u>Danny</u> – You. Boyd. Balcony. GOOD LAWD.<br><u>Ryan</u> – God, I could not adore you more than I do. Mine, mine, MINE!!!!! *SQUEEEEEZZZZEEEE*<br><u>Kassian</u> – Man, I hope you find true love…you need it.<br><u>Emilio</u> – You have a standing invitation to any party I ever have…ever.<br><u>Zach</u> – Finally. Sheesh. But, man, it took banging Viv to get there? Yuck.<br><br>With 6 chapters left, anything can happen. But at this point…I’m am <b>SO, SO, RIDICULOUSLY SATISFIED</b>. I’m looking at the final 6 as the epilogue… :)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16384750873652064525">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happe</span>
  <span id="freeText16384750873652064525" style="display:none">I know many are removing their ratings and reviews of all the books they have read, written by Santino Hassell, in light of his despicable behavior. I have deleted my ratings from all Santino books I have read, because I too am shocked and appalled!!! I won't do it with the ICOS series though. I am gonna be honest here and say, that this series is one of the best I have ever read, and I am sure Ais played a big part in my enjoyment. As far as I know, Ais had nothing to do with all that has happend. Until I hear otherwise, my ratings and reviews for this series, will stay up. I am sorry for those who might not agree with me on this. I would also like to say that I am so sorry for all of you who have been hurt....my heart goes out to all of you ;) xoxo<br><br><br>Re-read 7/15/17....cried my eyes out again....so so good !!!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/90s-crying-titanic-zombieland-woody-harrelson_zpsmbtfb7p8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467827950ra/19635556.gif" alt=" photo 90s-crying-titanic-zombieland-woody-harrelson_zpsmbtfb7p8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Damn these books...they are awesome but I am such a wreck right now. I'm so happy I made it, and so sad that it's done at the same time.<br><br>Once again, I am not going into the plot. There is no point to do so, because this is book 4 and it can't be read as a stand alone, so those of you who are going to read this one, will already know what and whom it's about. Also, I do not want to spoiler anything.<br><br>What I can tell you however, is that this series, even though harsh and gruesome and sad and frustrating, is about true love. Now don't go into this series, expecting roses and sunshine and romance...hell don't even go into it, if you hate your main characters to be with other people. There are other women and other men. <br><br>Also Boyd and Sin are not the only characters with a pov. This book is also about other people and their relationships. What stands out to me most though is that it is about real soulmates who need to be together. But it has never been said that true love is an easy love.... I seriously fell in love with Boyd and Sin.<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/True-Love-yhj984dc85_zpsl05jtot7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467827950ra/19635557.gif" alt=" photo True-Love-yhj984dc85_zpsl05jtot7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I liked all 4 books and I gave all of them 5 stars !! They are so intense !! They also have the best side characters ever. Some you will love and some you will hate, and your feelings about them will change time and again. I already expressed my love for Boyd and Sin, but there is another character, I want to exclaim my love for....Emilio... Man you are one sick bastard, but your heart is in the right place and I absolutely adore your filthy ass !! He also starred one of my favorite scenes in this book. Now I don't want to spoiler anything, so I will just use a gif ;) Those of you who've read the book, will know what I mean, those of you who haven't....read the books and pay attention :) Thank you Emilio, for that scene and making me feel better !!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/aanstekers-067_zpsjuhihfan.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467827950ra/19635558.gif" alt=" photo aanstekers-067_zpsjuhihfan.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So now that I'm done with reading about 5000 pages, I will probably fall into the black hole of a bookslump ;) Doesn't matter, it was worth it and eventhough I really hate saying goodbye to my new best friends...I know I will always be able to visit them again with a re-read :)<br><br>Thank you Sin and Boyd, you guys rock !! And thank you to my personal support system Susan, for listening to my whining, while I read these !!!<br><br><a href="http://s172.photobucket.com/user/Wendy_Ciliacus/media/tumblr_mv28q4Ss3U1sk816ro1_500_zpsrtkx2lxr.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467827950ra/19635559.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mv28q4Ss3U1sk816ro1_500_zpsrtkx2lxr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16384750873652064525" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9002678194364833912">I’ve just read this for the second time and if anything I enjoyed it even more this time. This book is incredible, it has everything including humour for which I have to thank Emilio.<br/><br/>Original review.<br/><br/>Absolutely amazingly brilliant.<br/><br/>I read a lot of books and I've been fortunate enough read some really great ones plus a lot of not-so-great ones as well but this has to be without a doubt the best, most addictive and compulsive series I've ever read. <br/>It's amazing and the fact that I've 5 starred every</span>
  <span id="freeText9002678194364833912" style="display:none">I’ve just read this for the second time and if anything I enjoyed it even more this time. This book is incredible, it has everything including humour for which I have to thank Emilio.<br /><br />Original review.<br /><br />Absolutely amazingly brilliant.<br /><br />I read a lot of books and I've been fortunate enough read some really great ones plus a lot of not-so-great ones as well but this has to be without a doubt the best, most addictive and compulsive series I've ever read. <br />It's amazing and the fact that I've 5 starred every book tells you something because I don't give 5* easily or often.<br />After 'Interludes' I was very apprehensive about starting this and it took comments from several friends before I found the courage to start.<br />My problem was Boyd's mission, I assumed this book would run with that and I wasn't sure I could cope with reading it. It didn't and I was so grateful for about a minute and then.....<br />Seriously these books should come with a warning (and a bottle or two of wine) it was so much worse than I expected and yet so much better.<br />We still get Boyd's mission retrospectively and that's bad enough but the rest OMG the rest.....<br /><br />I don't want to give anything away or spoil it in anyway so I'm not saying more about the story itself.<br />I can't begin to describe how incredible I found this book and this series, it's taken over my life even when I'm not reading I'm thinking about the characters and the story, I've become totally obsessed with Sin and Boyd. <br />I still have '1/27 An ICoS Anthology' yet to read and then I'm not sure what I'll do and how I'll move on from here.<br />While this is the end (tears and heartbreak here) of In The Company Of Shadows I'm hoping for more, the book ended but it can be picked up again and I'm seriously hoping it is it would be a shame to not continue this it would also be a shame for this not to reach a larger audience. <br />I am so grateful that I have friends who've read this and their reviews pointed me in its direction, I'd never have found it otherwise.<br />This series is unforgettable.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer234319931" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18196102014229116270">The best in the series, and the most disturbing, heartbreaking, pull your hair out, weep in agony <i>and</i> joy, God please let me not love & worry about all of these characters, fuck it I'm losing sleep again book...ever. <br/><br/>You can argue till the death about these characters, and I really feel no one is wrong. Why? Because they are so realistically written. They aren't pretty, they will piss you off, they will make you cry, and all along you just want something wonderful to happen...and then, it does. </span>
  <span id="freeText18196102014229116270" style="display:none">The best in the series, and the most disturbing, heartbreaking, pull your hair out, weep in agony <i>and</i> joy, God please let me not love &amp; worry about all of these characters, fuck it I'm losing sleep again book...ever. <br /><br />You can argue till the death about these characters, and I really feel no one is wrong. Why? Because they are so realistically written. They aren't pretty, they will piss you off, they will make you cry, and all along you just want something wonderful to happen...and then, it does. These books and men are violent, extremely violent. They make descisions that are careless. They make descisions with too much thought put into them. They hurt the ones they love on purpose and sometimes on accident. They are individuals in denial with too much awareness of the world around them. They grow up along the way in painful ways and some of them never grow up. What they live up to isnt often who they are. They love with ever fiber in their being, can be selfish beyond understanding, often cant understand others, have hopes and dreams, and live every day in full color. There aren't many characters out there that can compare. <br /><br />I adore them, I've loved every second of the reader bonding this series brings out, the discussions, the friendships made, and the memories I'll <i>always</i> hold dear. Thank you Sonny &amp; Ais for writing this amazing series. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18196102014229116270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2785238925" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2785238925" />
    <a title="Ms. Smartarse" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13703358-ms-smartarse"><img alt="Ms. Smartarse" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1401273675p2/13703358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2785238925?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ms. Smartarse" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ms. Smartarse" href="/user/show/13703358-ms-smartarse">Ms. Smartarse</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Ms. Smartarse by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/27899735-dia">Dia</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=action-adventure">action-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=part_of_a_series">part_of_a_series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=murder">murder</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=perfect-ending">perfect-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=rave">rave</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=psychological">psychological</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13703358-ms-smartarse?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2785238925" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2285355572300363959">After the rather ominous ending of the prequel, I felt ready to jump into Boyd's lengthy undercover mission, and yearn alongside him for the much anticipated reunion with Hsin... but the authors had a completely different idea about that. They skipped right through <em>those</em> particular horrors, and straight into the utter despair of a changed home life.<br/><br/>When I say that a book made me cry, I normally think of a few sniffles I let loose at the end, generally at the expense of children or animals suffer</span>
  <span id="freeText2285355572300363959" style="display:none">After the rather ominous ending of the prequel, I felt ready to jump into Boyd's lengthy undercover mission, and yearn alongside him for the much anticipated reunion with Hsin... but the authors had a completely different idea about that. They skipped right through <em>those</em> particular horrors, and straight into the utter despair of a changed home life.<br><br>When I say that a book made me cry, I normally think of a few sniffles I let loose at the end, generally at the expense of children or animals suffering. In here, I was in full on sob-fest for the duration of the first 200+ pages, and still felt the need for the occasional encore later on. Since I read an average of about 50 pages/hour, I'm sure you can appreciate the lovely Sunday I've been having. <em>Yes</em>, I'm that slow... moreso when things get depressing.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556731277ra/27441216.gif" alt="So many feelings" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I resorted to reading reviews, to try and assure myself that things couldn't possibly be at their worst... only to quickly move back to reading the actual book, for fear of spoilers. When the oppressive depression got too bad, I considered mixing things up with some feel-good fanfiction of what-if scenarios from Vermont, but my mind kept being pulled back into Boyd's inevitably bleak, if surprisingly determined, present mindset.<br><br>In essence, this book felt like one big package of a never ending list of unfairness, starting with the new Marshall, ending with Vivian Beaulieu's raison d'être, and interspersed with every single one of Boyd's anguished screams. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1556730512ra/27441163.gif" alt="this isn't fair" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>... so I totally had to come back later, to reread all those shmexy and fluffy scenes I was too stressed to properly appreciate before.<br><br><strong>Score: 4.7/5 stars</strong><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/48694-in-the-company-of-shadows" title="In the Company of Shadows" rel="nofollow noopener">ICoS</a> was such a contradictory series for me. On the one hand it has all the writing pet-peeves that I ran away from in M/F stories, and it's depressing enough to be perpetually illustrated by wind-swept, and rain-soaked greyscale GIFs.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1538521547ra/26391781.gif" alt="Stitch crying in the rain" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But at the same time, it's also a love story between two wonderful, broken and incredibly twisted men, that has kept me obsessed for a month a half now. Despite the insane amount of pain, suffering and overall unfair situations that Boyd and Hsin are constantly thrown into, I could weather through them all, knowing that there would be a final scene, with them riding off into the sunset. What can I say: I'm such a sucker for the happily-ever-after.<br><br>====================<br>Review of vol1 of book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2159457466" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall: Volume 1: Director's Cut</a><br>Review of vol2 of book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2160490850" rel="nofollow noopener">Evenfall: Volume 2: Director's Cut</a><br>Review of book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2750521621" rel="nofollow noopener">Afterimage</a><br>Review of book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2780757393" rel="nofollow noopener">The Interludes</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2285355572300363959" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_803725910" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/803725910" />
    <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b"><img alt="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374929701p2/3716081.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/803725910?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b">It&#39;s just me Shelly B</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer803725910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12115647835259881680"><b>I'm so sad because I never wanted this to end I could read about these characters forever!!! I am in LOVE with series and I can't believe it's OVER!!! <br/><br/><br/>I just cant believe it's over......CONSUMED these books consumed ME!! Im guessing here, on the length of this series, but 4000+ pages and I'm pissed because I can't wake up tomorrow and read MORE!! This should never end.....yes I'm a greedy bitch and I don't CARE!!<br/></b><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Hsin "Sin"</u>
</b><br/>Oh my sweet psychotic Hsin.....you stole my heart!!! I will never forg</span>
  <span id="freeText12115647835259881680" style="display:none"><b>I'm so sad because I never wanted this to end I could read about these characters forever!!! I am in LOVE with series and I can't believe it's OVER!!! <br /><br /><br />I just cant believe it's over......CONSUMED these books consumed ME!! Im guessing here, on the length of this series, but 4000+ pages and I'm pissed because I can't wake up tomorrow and read MORE!! This should never end.....yes I'm a greedy bitch and I don't CARE!!<br /></b><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Hsin "Sin"</u>
</b><br />Oh my sweet psychotic Hsin.....you stole my heart!!! I will never forget you....you are the tragic hero that people will either love or hate. I say screw the ones who hate because now you know who you are and you are beautifully flawed! You were dealt such a shitty hand but you let him in and it was so wonderful and painful watching it all unfold. You are also a badass f*cker and to answer a question in the book.........YES your strength would turn anyone on!!! Bruise me....toss me around....use me like a PUPPET...I don't care!! But he loves you and I love the way he loves you so I'm gonna have to step back and be the bigger person here.....sorry but that's just the way it is:)<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Boyd</u>
</b><br />Damn boy you REALLY grew up through this series!! I didn't like you much at first because quite frankly I thought you were just an emo punk but you have WOWED me since book 1. Your devotion and love for, not just for Hsin, but for everyone you deem trustworthy is beautiful!! The pain you felt in the first part of book4 killed me......I almost cried and I don't cry when I read!!! The fact that you didn't give up and had the tenacity to overcome it was so endearing to me! I love you like a brother but Im so jealous of you!!! I want them green eyes staring at ME not YOU!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Emilio</u>
</b><br />OMG YOU bastard.....I LOVE YOU!!!! I love everything you say everything you do!!! I want to hang out with YOU!! If I could rip a character out of a book I think it would be you!!! You are like a bulldog on a bone when you get something in your mind, you could careless what anyone thinks about you....the sarcasm, the insults, the devotion, the love.......I love YOU!!! You might be a slut but who cares.....well I know one who might care;). Mwahhhhhhh my Emilio I will never forget you!!!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Zachary</u>
</b><br />Stoic and steadfast! You always stood by the ones you loved even when it was tough love. I didn't always agree with your decisions in the beginning but looking back you did it out of love! If everyone could have someone like you in their life the world would be a great place. I wish you wouldn't have f*cked with my mans head so much but I'm willing to over look it because I knew through out it all you had everyone's best interest at hand.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Kassian </u>
</b><br />Damn you.....I hated you for awhile but in reality you helped calm the storm. I loved all the controversy you brought on all sides but seriously dude remember to turn the comm unit off next time!!!!!!!!!! You are alright with now though.....you always came thru when someone needed you;)<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Ryan</u>
</b><br />I want to pinch your cheeks!!!!!!!! Love love love you!!!! You knew who was important from the beginning and your loyalty astounds me......precious and trustworthy is all I can say.....everyone needs a friend like you!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Vivienne</u>
</b><br />You are a BITCH....no one should treat their child that way! Because of the ending I understand your logic, but it doesn't excuse it! If you would have shown him a little bit of love he would have been completely loyal to you.....well I guess at times you did show a small modicum of love but when I say small I mean SMALL! Anyway you came through in the end so you get a few points from me.<br /><br /><br /> <b>
  <u>Owen</u>
</b><br />You crazy weirdo take a NAP!!! Jesus I don't know what to think about you....hell I still don't know what to think about you!! You did crack me up though!!!! The shit you said was ridiculous and funny but I just never knew where your loyalties lie and I still don't know but you made laugh so I'll give you a pass.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Jeffery</u>
</b><br />Meh.....that's all I'm saying about him! He always seemed shady to me.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Ivan</u>
</b><br />Meh......that's all I'm saying about him! If you read it. You'll understand!<br /><br /><br /><br />There's so many more characters but I'm not going into them all.....I just hit the highlights above.<br /><br />There aren't many series where even the "supposedly" secondary characters really matter to me but that wasn't the case here.....no matter who was in the spotlight I loved IT!!! In the end though everyone had a role to play so I'm not sure if they should even be called secondary characters because they all played a part!! <br /><br /><br /> Nothing ever went as planned and you were always left with the feeling of "WTF will happen next," I secretly love that feeling!!!!!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Breakdown Book by Book</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>Book 1</b> - Damn that was good!!! I mean REALLY GOOD!!!!! Wow!!!! Oh shit I'm in love these characters!!<br /><br /><b>Book 2 </b> - OMG I can't believe it......I'm in love with this series.....I can't stop.....I have to continue.....I don't want this to end......I'm obsessed....but I can't stop!!!!! Life around me is continuing but all I can do is read!!!<br /><br /><b>Book 3 </b>- And the PLOT thickens......oh shit I'm getting ready to start the last book!!! I have to draw it out because I don't want this to end!!!!<br /><br /><b>Book 4</b> - OH shittttttttt! This book is good and sad and my emotions are all over the place!!!!! Oh no I'm finished I want to cry....it can't be over!!! Noooooooooooooooo it can't be.......I need more....I want more....nnooooooooooooooooo! <br /><br /><br /><br />OMG I'm rambling!!! However this series is by far one of the BEST I've ever read....at work I thought about it.....at home I thought about it.....during conversations I thought about it...listening to music I thought about it.....I told my husband not to talk me bc I couldn't stop.....he was ready to strangle me....by the way remember 4000+ pages yea he was ready to kill me.....the point of this is......<br /><br /><br /><b>DO NOT READ THIS SERIES UNLESS YOU ARE READY TO BE CONSUMED!!! BECAUSE IT WILL CONSUME EVERY THOUGHT YOU HAVE!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1201260655" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201260655" />
    <a title="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15615404-tara-mindforbooks"><img alt="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1547115831p2/15615404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1201260655?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tara♥ {MindforBooks}" href="/user/show/15615404-tara-mindforbooks">Tara♥ {MindforBooks}</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=2015-books">2015-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=mm">mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=heroes-i-love">heroes-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=favourites-2015">favourites-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15615404-tara-mindforbooks?shelf=lickable-males">lickable-males</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201260655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13870981590151428773"><br/><b>"A dismal end to lives forever cast in shadow."</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426251457i/13992806.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If I could use only one word to describe ‘Fade’ that word would be <b>PAIN</b>. <br/><br/>‘Fade’ ripped me apart, had me ugly crying regularly, so much so that I had puffy eyes for about two days straight which led to people constantly asking me if I was okay. It necessitated the very first ‘Irish ICoS Support Group’ being set up and it basically took over my life completely for 9 days. <br/><br/>So yeah pain. But it was a beautiful kind of pain. <br/><br/>This series was a fabulous ex</span>
  <span id="freeText13870981590151428773" style="display:none"><br><b>"A dismal end to lives forever cast in shadow."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426251457i/13992806.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I could use only one word to describe ‘Fade’ that word would be <b>PAIN</b>. <br><br>‘Fade’ ripped me apart, had me ugly crying regularly, so much so that I had puffy eyes for about two days straight which led to people constantly asking me if I was okay. It necessitated the very first ‘Irish ICoS Support Group’ being set up and it basically took over my life completely for 9 days. <br><br>So yeah pain. But it was a beautiful kind of pain. <br><br>This series was a fabulous experience. The characters (good and pure evil) are going to be staying with me for a long, long time to come. Hsin and Boyd’s relationship was an epic one. The two of them together was so wonderful and so intense, the two of them apart was soul destroying.<br><br><b>”He lost connection with everything except the agony that burrowed a seed down into his heart.”</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426251457ra/13992807.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>“Why did he always have to be the one left behind? Why did he always have to be the one to gather the broken pieces and glue them back together, a mockery of what he'd once been? Why did he always have to suffer through the loss—that gaping, wrenching loss that sucked him up, ripped him apart, and carelessly threw him aside?"</b><br><br>The places Hsin and Boyd go in this book were so surprising and as painful as the journey they took was, it was also extraordinary. It makes me giddy and distraught just thinking about them in Annadale. It felt to me that no matter what, no matter the obstacles that were placed in their path they would find each other. Together they would overcome everything. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426078022i/13971032.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Boyd’s pain was palpable at times throughout this. There were times in the series that myself and Boyd fell out. I tried to look at things from his point of view many times and most of the time I understood why he did what he did. That was until a certain foot message which caused me to have a totally irrational meltdown. After that we drifted apart for a little but all was forgiven in this. ‘Fade’ is mostly Boyd’s POV and it was just incredible, he will now forever be on my ‘heroes I love’ shelf (along with Hsin and Emilio of course) and being with him through some really awful events and some truly beautiful ones was one of the best reading experiences I’ve ever had.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426251536i/13992813.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>“Freedom is not worth it without him. I don’t remember everything, but I know that.”</b><br><br>I am so sad to be finished ICoS. It is such an addictive series and one of the best I’ve ever read. For 31 days I obsessed, I cried, I laughed, I screamed, I fell in love and I fell in hate with the characters in this world. I met wonderful people on Twitter, here and in RL because of it. I dreamt of it every night and when I wasn’t reading it I was staring off into space thinking about it. I have no idea what to do with myself now. I feel kind of lost. Thanking Ais and Sonny for this seems so inadequate. It still boggles my mind that this is free, it’s an amazing gift and one I will be forever grateful for. <br><br><b>”It’s because the truth is important. Never let anyone tell you differently, Boyd. Even if it hurts to say, even if it’s painful to hear, even if you wish you could run the other way – it’s important. It separates the people with integrity from the deceivers. It’s what makes a person trustworthy. Somebody to believe in. “</b> <br><br>So onwards we go. I’m excited about what’s next. <br><br><b>”But that was the way it went anytime a person was on the precipice of change. The fear of the future mixed with the loss of the past. At those times, all a person could do was step forward.”</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426161286ra/13982535.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13870981590151428773" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18009153795814573420"><b> BIGGEST 5 STARS IN THE WHOLE UNIVERSE for this REMARKABLE, PHENOMENAL, ASTONISHING, WONDERFUL, AWESOME BOOK that is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11737700.Fade__In_the_company_of_shadows___4_' title='Fade (In the company of shadows, #4) by Santino Hassell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fade</a> <br/><br/>ABSOLUTELY MARVELLOUS!!! </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456089592ra/18188746.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Question: </b> <i> How can you describe THE BEST BOOK you've read so far? How can you describe the last book in the most AMAZING series in the world? And I am talking here about a series that kept me up for so many nights and consumed me so much!!! </i><br/><br/><b> Answer: </b> <i> You just can't find the perfect words! Stop trying to... There are no words to do it justice... unf</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18009153795814573420" style="display:none"><b> BIGGEST 5 STARS IN THE WHOLE UNIVERSE for this REMARKABLE, PHENOMENAL, ASTONISHING, WONDERFUL, AWESOME BOOK that is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11737700.Fade__In_the_company_of_shadows___4_" title="Fade (In the company of shadows, #4) by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">Fade</a> <br><br>ABSOLUTELY MARVELLOUS!!! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456089592ra/18188746.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Question: </b> <i> How can you describe THE BEST BOOK you've read so far? How can you describe the last book in the most AMAZING series in the world? And I am talking here about a series that kept me up for so many nights and consumed me so much!!! </i><br><br><b> Answer: </b> <i> You just can't find the perfect words! Stop trying to... There are no words to do it justice... unfortunately. </i> <br><br>It was very hard for me to start to write this review. <br>Sometimes it's hard for me to write about a book I didn't like. But I never expected to be so difficult searching for words to describe a book that I absolutely loved! <br>Well it seems I can't find my words when I try to describe anything related to this series. Maybe because I already know that anything I write will somehow ruin it's pure beauty... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465335135ra/19342289.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't want to give too much away. Josy is still reading it. So enjoy it my dear and I don't want to ruin any of the surprises! :)<br><br>I on the other hand, I begged so much for some spoilers, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ especially when Carhart was shot and I was asking frantically if he really died because my heart almost stopped!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but ***Ralu*** is such a good friend and didn't want to ruin it for me, so she didn't say a word! So, thank you Ralu!!! <br><br>It was awesome to discover this last book. It was so different from what I imagined...<br><br>I must add some spoilers. Seems like I just can't keep it to myself: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br>I really thought the book will start with Boyd's mission. I was wrong! :)<br>I thought Boyd will discover Danny in one of his missions, but his termination being his assignment. Nope again. ;)<br>I thought Boyd will tell Danny the truth... But no, no, no. <br>None of the things I imagined happened in the book. And I am very happy!!! I hate when I can picture the end of a book.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So this book was NOT predictable. At all! This is one of the many reasons I think it is the best.<br><br>It was so much more than I expected and after 3 wonderful books I expected A LOT. But I just couldn't imagine any of the things that actually happened. <br><br>The first half of the book made me ache, SO BAD! But I just couldn't accept it. Pure and simple! So I waited for the things to fit in place... without any patience left in my bones... BUT IT WAS WORTH IT! The waiting.<br>Oh boy, any time I thought everything was about to settle down, it was just the silence before the storm... AND the beginning of another chapter FULL OF ACTION AND SUSPENSE. Of course. It's ICoS after all!!!<br><br>Well I wish I could write more but I won't because I learned on my own skin that it is better to discover yourself all the goodies in the books. <br><br><b> And ICoS is just too perfect to try to analyze more. It has so many KEY points and so many characters you learned to love - Emilio and Carhart, but Kassian too. GOD, I MISS THEM ALREADY!!! <br><br>If you read the book/series you know what I'm talking about. If you didn't ... well, you really, really, really have to read ICoS!!!<br><br>And I also feel the need to thank to Sonny and Ais for this precious, oh so precious gift that is this PERFECT series! <br><br>Can't wait to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20927491.1_27_An_ICoS_Anthology" title="1/27 An ICoS Anthology by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">1/27: An ICoS Anthology</a>!!! </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462793274i/19043945._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_633150624" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/633150624" />
    <a title="SueC" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9057957-suec"><img alt="SueC" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357037447p2/9057957.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/633150624?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueC" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueC" href="/user/show/9057957-suec">SueC</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9057957-suec?shelf=i-will-love-you-forever">i-will-love-you-forever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9057957-suec?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer633150624" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5940384548874975376"><b>You know that terrible sinking feeling you get when you realize that the alternate universe you've been living in (and loving) has just finished? Yep, I'm feeling it post Fade... but it's completely worth it.</b><br/><br/>Here's the thing with 'In the Company of Shadows': it's long. It's so long that there were times when I rolled my eyes and felt like all the teeny tiny details were completely unnecessary... BUT they weren't. The details and inner ramblings served their purpose in helping us love and underst</span>
  <span id="freeText5940384548874975376" style="display:none"><b>You know that terrible sinking feeling you get when you realize that the alternate universe you've been living in (and loving) has just finished? Yep, I'm feeling it post Fade... but it's completely worth it.</b><br /><br />Here's the thing with 'In the Company of Shadows': it's long. It's so long that there were times when I rolled my eyes and felt like all the teeny tiny details were completely unnecessary... BUT they weren't. The details and inner ramblings served their purpose in helping us love and understand the characters and their predicaments. <br /><br />The most interesting thing and what I can't seem to fathom is how the authors managed to navigate this plot. I mean, it is an immensely complicated tapestry of clues, characters and events. It's genius and with each page you turn the plot just thickens.<br /><br />The characters were awesome and so well developed. Some were instantly lovable, while others were incredibly despicable. At the same time, all were intriguing (and a few a worthy of their own stand-alone books). There's an amazing point where the authors managed to convey a clear shift in personality when one of the characters 'changes' from one moment to the next. You could <i>feel</i> the difference in persona immediately. Just. So. Clever. <br /><br />The authors were kind enough to give us an extra sensory stimulus where a soundtrack song is noted to accompany a particular scene/chapter. It was the freaken bomb. There were parts of the story which had me feeling like I'd literally lost my breath. Parts where you could feel the tension rising to Defcon 1 or alternatively a plot twist that smacks you in the face and knocks you off your feet without any chance of seeing it coming.<br /><br />So at the very end of this amazing journey (around 4,500 pages) I wanted to get off my numb bum and give this story a standing ovation. Really, it was that good.<br /><br />Oh, and by the way, I'm a Vega Lover. I'll wear the t-shirt and use the mug 'cause them Vegas are totes hot.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5940384548874975376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1760229280" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760229280" />
    <a title="Cristopher" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6450354-cristopher"><img alt="Cristopher" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470190319p2/6450354.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1760229280?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristopher" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristopher" href="/user/show/6450354-cristopher">Cristopher</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6450354-cristopher?shelf=five-star-books">five-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1760229280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8536474555404630392"><b>All of those stars in the sky. All of those.</b><br/><br/>I can't believe its the end.<br/><br/>I'm a little mess here. I didn't want it to end. And I fucking hate it when it's time to finally say goodbye. It's just a bit heavy in the chest you know? Being attached, protective, caring and in love with the characters and all that shit. And yet.. At the end of it all, you still have to say bye. Sigh.<br/><br/>Sorry, I'm pathetic I know, it's embarrassing. But whatever. ='(<br/><br/>***<br/><br/>How do you describe a book this good? I can't think of a</span>
  <span id="freeText8536474555404630392" style="display:none"><b>All of those stars in the sky. All of those.</b><br /><br />I can't believe its the end.<br /><br />I'm a little mess here. I didn't want it to end. And I fucking hate it when it's time to finally say goodbye. It's just a bit heavy in the chest you know? Being attached, protective, caring and in love with the characters and all that shit. And yet.. At the end of it all, you still have to say bye. Sigh.<br /><br />Sorry, I'm pathetic I know, it's embarrassing. But whatever. ='(<br /><br />***<br /><br />How do you describe a book this good? I can't think of any way. I can only speak of my experience..<br /><br />So here goes..<br /><br />This has put me into some kind of intense pain. That kind when you have to just sit down, close your eyes and try to practice deep breathing..<br /><br />I can't believe how at point, how meticulous and how successful the writing of this is.. It definitely has the <b>most accurate and saddest scenes to be ever written in a book</b>. It just painted the pain vividly and you can't help but feel the devastating hollowness the characters are going through. I still could feel it even now when I think about it. It's really a glorious, beautiful sadness that could bring tears.<br /><br />Now I don't wanna scare people who haven't read it yet. But believe me, it's totally, totally worth it. You wouldn't wanna miss the most accurate written form of the emotion when you lose someone that important. (my own opinion 'course.)<br /><br />That moment in the beach? Watching the sunset, Boyd sitting down far from Sin. It just really breaks me. I dont know why.. But it pictured soo much. How much Boyd cared for the guy, how in love he was.. That he was ready to do whatever it is to make Sin happy. Even at his expense, even if it hurts him. I can't believe he's the same guy I hated so much in book 2. <br /><br />Then the boat ride watching the dark sky full of stars. Them holding each other as they make their way to freedom, thinking of the first time they met 6 years ago. I swear I had to play the song "Wait" by M83 while reading that scene. And the effect was surreal. Had me closing to tears.<br /><br />This - obvious to my updates - have earned from me unquantifiable amount of "Oh My God!!" "Holy sheesh." "What the freak?!" "What the hell?!" "Foooking animal!" And many more sick expressions in my language. LOL! <b>The twists and turns of the plot are just purely genius</b>. This series has seriously mastered the art of flooring me. One moment things are fine, easy and steady.. The next I'm being swirled, caught by a damn tornado. It was insane.<br /><br />It made me love even the side characters so much. That I wanna scream when bad things would happen to them. But also made me laugh at little funny things they say or do. I want them all to have their own books!!! Especially Emilio and Carhart.<br /><br />All this time I thought I love Sin more than Boyd.. But Boyd, have completely, truly managed to change that. Now I love them equally. And unsurprisingly, they are now in the same ranks of my most favorite couples: Ty&amp;Zane, Dan&amp;Vadim, Boyd&amp;Sin.<br /><br />I know how vague this review is.. But this is that kind of book where you just have to go in blind and let it surprise you. It just worked best for me that way. Plus, im a bit of a mess with the series coming to an end, so vague is really what you gonna get.<br /><br />I know too.. That no matter how much I blab in here, I wouldn't be able to give a justified review to this great, great book.<br /><br />Of course I also know that this is getting long. So I have to cut it short now and get on to the anthology.<br /><br />It really makes me deeply sad that I'm only a short book away to really saying goodbye to this wonderful characters. But well.. Sigh. I shouldn't have let myself get too attached.. But that's impossible. <b>They are among the most tragic, flawed, beautiful characters I've ever had the chance to read..</b><br /><br />***<br /><br />Anyway, these are my soundtrack for this one hell of an epic book:<br /><br />"To Build A Home" by Cinematic Orchestra<br />"Wait" by M83<br />"Sedated" by Hozier<br />"Dont You Remember" by Adele<br />"Cavalier" by James Vincent McMorrow<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8536474555404630392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2048503602" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2048503602" />
    <a title="Virginia Cavanillas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19380470-virginia-cavanillas"><img alt="Virginia Cavanillas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556819327p2/19380470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2048503602?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Cavanillas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Cavanillas" href="/user/show/19380470-virginia-cavanillas">Virginia Cavanillas</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=lgtb">lgtb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=rambles">rambles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19380470-virginia-cavanillas?shelf=sci-fi-romance">sci-fi-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2048503602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10651847480243532563">Rating removed because of this:<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh'>http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br/><br/>Ais you rock!<br/><br/>Original review:<br/><br/>I've been so immersed in this <b>epic story</b>, so... living their lives in this futuristic post apocalyptic reality that now that it has ended, <b>I feel empty</b>. With that distressful feeling you have every time you end something you know you won't forget. Characters that keep coming to your mind, unforgettable quotes burning your brain and so many feels all around...*sighs loudly while trying not to cry*<br/><br/>B</span>
  <span id="freeText10651847480243532563" style="display:none">Rating removed because of this:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statement-on-sh">http://riptidepublishing.com/a-statem...</a><br><br>Ais you rock!<br><br>Original review:<br><br>I've been so immersed in this <b>epic story</b>, so... living their lives in this futuristic post apocalyptic reality that now that it has ended, <b>I feel empty</b>. With that distressful feeling you have every time you end something you know you won't forget. Characters that keep coming to your mind, unforgettable quotes burning your brain and so many feels all around...*sighs loudly while trying not to cry*<br><br>Before I start with my rambling and promising to keep it short and as spoiler free as I can manage,  I have something to say. <br>Both authors (BOTH) did an amazing job creating this sci-fi universe full of awesome and so-worked little things. The characters (and I'm not referring just to my Hsin and Boyd. All of them) are deep and incredibly detailed. I know I've said it before but <b>ICoS is a masterpiece. Imperfect and unedited</b> but a masterpiece after all. <br>This is a work that deserves recognition and to be more known. <b>The world building is delightful but the writing too and so loaded with emotion, humor and depth</b>.<br>Santino is pretty known now and I've enjoyed his other books (although I've been told I have the best of them pending) but I can't compare any of the books I've read with this one. With Hsin. With this love story. With the secondary characters.) <br>So kudos to Santino for his collaboration creating this marvelous series and <b>a special and personal message to Ais:</b> you are the shit, girl! As simple as that. What a skilled writer you are and <b>what a beautiful character you've created. Boyd is deep, complex, brave and his is one of the most astonishing evolutions ever</b>. Amazing job. He supports the first 20% of this book without any help and he drives the rest as the champ he is. Fade is undoubtedly his book. There is too much work behind this blondie and this is something that must be said. <br><br>And now, with that out of my system, I'll just say, <b>this book is 1214 pages of wonderfulness. The best book in the series</b> IMO, the book I've been needing since I read Afterimage and I was bored and a bit depressed. The interludes worked wonderfully but this one? Just wow.<br>The beginning of Fade is rough tough. It goes direct to the suffering.  You can feel Boyd's loneliness, his angst, the complete emptiness he is feeling. Pure devastation and so, so well written that you can almost touch the cold, the edge of desperation. The way it cuts.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509995309i/24377275.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[My poor thing goes through drugs, abuse and  rape, to finally come "home" and realize he is alone. Without the love of this life. Without his reason to keep going. What a brave thing he is. <br>That first encounter with Emilio... I was crying like a baby even if I knew it couldn't be possible for Hsin to be dead, but still... so painful and spectacularly narrated. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>"Color fading from the world like a watercolor painting left out in the rain"</b>
</i><br><br><b>The way Fade is told is heaven, being Boyd the real star shining through his overwhelming feelings</b> but, at the same time, not shadowing the rest of the story and characters. He is the indiscutible pillar here but we also have a good mystery going on and terrific secondary stories conducting and linking the main plot. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[My special fav: Emilio and Zack. I've been a fan from the beginning but here I was ecstatic, wanting more of them, excited, eager, nervous. It's rough and addictive and it comes on page in the right and perfect moments. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I won't give away anything about the plot. I'll just say the precarious freedom the characters have live in from the beginning has its culmination in this book.<b> In Fade the show is live</b>. Santino &amp; Ais  transmit magnificently the claustrophobic situation our guys are in, the false freedom the agency gives them under the constant menace of termination. They have to obey or they are dead. And now the ones who keep breathing are simply trying to survive and deal with the situation the best they can. Keeping secrets, hiding, carving out weird alliances and friendships.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Freedom is not worth it without him"</b>
</i><br><br>Kassian, Ryan, Zach... I can't even... so I'm not doing it. I think you get the idea of what my feelings are so I'll leave you alone with just a slight overview of my thoughts (if I enter full your are dead, believe me. The gates are open and my emotions are all over the place because I really loved Fade and the way is told)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509995309i/24377276.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>If you want a complete and intense reading experience, look no more. This is it.</b> Of course, it's not an easy ride. Far from it. ICoS is long at times (sooooo long, especially Afterimage) boring in some parts (except book one, the rest are unedited so you could find some scenes a bit too much, tedious even. Doesn't happen in Fade though, or not to me at least) but the journey deserves all the stars, all the praising and all the suffering they put you through because at the end all of it is worthwhile.<br><br>But It's not just the intense love story between Hsin and Boyd what made me fall hard for Fade, it's  the huge amount of <b>complex and attractive characters</b>, the <b>deep and well-done dialogues, the amazing background,  the main plot, the secondary ones joining and converging to create a perfect resolution. The atmosphere, the way the feelings are shown and not just told...</b> *sighs loudly* my emotions were out playing, kicking, shouting, crying and praying for a containment even if they didn't want for the awesomeness to stop *sighs again because explaining the whole thing is impossible*<br><br>So,<b> a highly recommend series with a more than awesome ending</b> where the love story is kinda a <i>reboot</i> where you can breath a super intense love story that knows very little frontiers.<br>Read it! Read the whole series when you have time and you won't regret it. <b>This story is gonna be with you, near you, following and haunting you for a long long time.</b> <br>And it's free so you have no excuse. I even leave you here the link to download it: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.inthecompanyofshadows.com/">http://www.inthecompanyofshadows.com/</a><br><br><a href="https://reviewsforbooklovers.blogspot.com.es/" rel="nofollow noopener">Reviews for Book Lovers</a><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503517262ra/23670232.gif" width="100" height="85" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_554604876" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/554604876" />
    <a title="Steph" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4215697-steph"><img alt="Steph" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346102450p2/4215697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/554604876?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph" href="/user/show/4215697-steph">Steph</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=kindle-read">kindle-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=provided-by-author">provided-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4215697-steph?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer554604876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10148670208011815331"> This book is completely devastating. It’s incredibly written as always, but it will tear you apart inside. For about the first 30%, I was very confused and was struggling to understand just what the hell had happened in the year that Boyd was away. <br/> Sin and Boyd had been so happy together but it seemed that this mission would finally be the last straw, the one thing that would have torn them apart, for good!<br/><br/> I have enjoyed this series more than I could have ever hoped, but I have to be honest, </span>
  <span id="freeText10148670208011815331" style="display:none"> This book is completely devastating. It’s incredibly written as always, but it will tear you apart inside. For about the first 30%, I was very confused and was struggling to understand just what the hell had happened in the year that Boyd was away. <br /> Sin and Boyd had been so happy together but it seemed that this mission would finally be the last straw, the one thing that would have torn them apart, for good!<br /><br /> I have enjoyed this series more than I could have ever hoped, but I have to be honest, this wasn't my favourite book at all. I have given this book the least stars in the series because I was so frustrated throughout most of it. It's nothing against the book itself, but anyone who knows me at all will know that I cannot stand memory loss stories, in any way, shape or form. I hate it. I was so disappointed when I realised that that's what was happening here. I then spent a huge part of the book being pretty annoyed. I wanted the memory loss story to be over, for things to get back on track where they were before. Seeing things this way just frustrated the hell out of me. I have never spent so long in a book, waiting for things to get better, to get the answers that we needed. I was so fed up of all the questions churning around in my head :(<br /><br /> ********************* Spoilers Ahead ********************<br /><br /><br /><br /> The twists and turns of the story were really great. I was so damn shocked by everything the Agency and the Reapers had done to Sin over the years. Everything was clicking so perfectly into place. Also, learning about the past and what really happened to Boyd's father, it was all so intriguing.<br /><br /> Boyd was wonderful in this book. His fortitude just made me love him even more. I admired just how well he dealt with everything and how strong he was. How he made some very hard decisions, to help others. <br /> Boyd and Sin and just as enthralling as they've always been, they have proved time and time again that they belong together and this book just cemented that fact. There is nothing in the world that could keep them apart.<br /> <br />'<i><b>"I love you, Hsin,"</b> he said hoarsely. <b>"I missed you so much."<br /> "I love you, too."</b> Sin's voice was still think and husky. <b>"I came back for you. Because I wanted to find you, because I wanted to remember you."</b><br /> Boyd let out a shuddering breath and hugged Sin harder.</i>'<br /><br /> Emilio completely stole my heart (yes, even more than he had already) in this book. I just adore him. I think he will always be one of my all-time favourite characters.<br /> I loved seeing all of his friendships develop more. Seeing him realise just how many people actually care about him and would be there for him when he needed them. I lost count of how many times he made me laugh, or something he said made me cry. He's just a truly incredible character.<br /><br /> <i>"I know you and blondie like to go all Joan of fucking Arc any chance you get, but let's rewind this shit a few weeks and break it down again before you decide all bets are off."</i><br /> LOL<br /><br /> The relationship between Boyd and Emilio was solidified in this book. I think going through such a traumatic time together really helped them bond. <br /><br /> Emilio and Zach were one of the true highlights of the entire book. I was desperate to see more, to harm or about their past and for them to finally work things out and be together. I liked that he never made it easy for Zach. After everything they've been through and just how much Emilio craves him, he still made Zach work his arse off until he would give him a chance. Rightly so I think. Zach has (although unintentionally) treated Emilio like dirt over the years and so I am glad he had to prove himself first.<br /> Seeing them finally get together was just amazing, they completely took my breath away, and not always in a good way. They are dark; they're dangerous and explosive, but it was the tiny little glimpses of tenderness and affection that made me love them even more…<br /><br /> <i><b>"All I know,"</b> he said finally, evenly. <b>"Is that you mean a lot to me. And no matter how many fucked up things you do, I keep coming back for more. So that must mean I care for you a lot."</b><br /> Emilio snickered. <b>"Well damn, don't get all mushy on me now. A simple 'You're my moon and stars, Emilio' would have sufficed."</b></i><br /> <br /> This one was also really sweet…<br /><br />'<i><b>"You ain't gonna try and hug me now, are you?"<br /> "No, but I did want to kiss you."</b> Carhart lifted his hand and wrapped it around one of Emilio's hard, tattooed shoulders. <b>"Is that okay, or is it too mushy for you?"</b><br /> Emilio finally cracked a smile, and he reached down to grasp one of the loops in Carhart’s jeans. He gave a tug, and pulled the general back towards the bed.'</i>'<br /><br /> This unfortunately brings me to another caomplaint of mine. I really didn't like the way things were left between them at the end. We left them in a life or death situation and never went back again. We were given tiny little hints as to what might have happened to them, or where they might be. But that wasn't enough for me, personally. I felt like their story just stopped mid-flow. There was no real ending or any kind of closure at all :(<br /><br /> Vivienne is, and will always be a monster. Even finally hearing the reasons for why she acts the way she does, I still didn't feel sorry for her at all. She’s a despicable human being.<br /><br /> Owen, Ryan, Kassian and the rest of the gang were great. I loved seeing them all again and they provided some seriously good laughs, especially the interactions between Owen, Boyd and Emilio.<br /><br /> <i><b>"Oh,"</b> Owen perked up. <b>"I'm glad you asked, Sir Sal. Maybe I'll make that your codename on this heist, by the way. You can be Sal, Emilio can be Crabs, and I'll be watchman. What do you think?"<br /> "I'm too pretty to have STD's."</b></i><br /><br /> Hahahaha.<br /><br /> I honestly wanted to cry when I finished this book, knowing it was likely things would never go any further. I felt like after everything we’ve been through with these characters, that the ending just didn't do them all justice.<br /> Everything I had expected to happen didn't. All of my hopes and dreams for them just didn't come true. And an offer from a creepy Agency guy really left me on edge. I didn’t like his offer at all. I just wanted Sin and Boyd to happy!<br /> But I still have so many questions I want answered. I just feel a little… sad, knowing that I will probably never get those answers.<br /> <br /><i>*Huge thanks to Giorgia and Em. For reading every single book together. It wouldn't have been the same without you.*</i></span>
