<div id="review_179715351" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/179715351" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/179715351?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=free-stuff">free-stuff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2295424-mel?shelf=on-line-fiction">on-line-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer179715351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11003533456562171251">*sniffle* <br/><br/>I just finished. Ugh, my mind is spinning with a wide variety of thoughts and feelings. And bittersweetness prevails. <br/>I can't believe this is the end. I can't believe this journey is over. But there it was, written in black and white italics: <i>'The End of In the Company of Shadows'</i>. <br/><br/>*sniffle*<br/><br/>With the last book of the series, it's really inevitable not to incorporate the series as a whole in the rating. And that general evaluation would lead to 5 stars. Which is weird, since I didn't act</span>
  <span id="freeText11003533456562171251" style="display:none">*sniffle* <br /><br />I just finished. Ugh, my mind is spinning with a wide variety of thoughts and feelings. And bittersweetness prevails. <br />I can't believe this is the end. I can't believe this journey is over. But there it was, written in black and white italics: <i>'The End of In the Company of Shadows'</i>. <br /><br />*sniffle*<br /><br />With the last book of the series, it's really inevitable not to incorporate the series as a whole in the rating. And that general evaluation would lead to 5 stars. Which is weird, since I didn't actually rate any of the other books 5 stars separately (4-4,5 stars). But the series as a whole was just superb, all encompassing, super engaging. Good plot, great world building, and characters you just can't seem to get out of your mind. The authors have no qualms with putting their characters through the wringer... again and again. And you're with them every agonizing step of the way. I was absorbed, squeeing, raving and right out fangirling at times. If that doesn't deserve a 5 star rating, then I don't know what does. <br /><br /><i>Fade</i> was the last part in this iCos journey and it was a fitting goodbye. It was good, it was emotional, it was dark, frustrating, infuriating and endearing. <br />There are some chapters that were absolute genius. Which had me cry my heart out, on the edge of my seat, and laughing out loud. Especially Boyd's homecoming had a profound effect on me. <br />Other than that, it was so good to see the old dynamics in the relationship between Sin and Boyd, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(something which was only underlined by Boyd's interaction with Danny) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and great to see new dynamics unfurling <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(Emilio and Carhart, yeah baby!) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br /><br />The ending was everything you'd expect and more. Pretty much all story lines were tied and everything came to blows, and it was chaos and madness and beautiful. <br />The epilogue was SUPERB! I have a dislike for epilogues since some authors tend to sap out in them, but this was the exact opposite of everything I hate in an epilogue. No perfect endings and pretty bows, but cautious happiness tempered by ambivalence, uneasiness and lingering doubts. And then: new opportunities but nothing being finalized. <br />It was a perfect point to stop, but it still leaves you wanting more (and more and more). <br /><br />This all being said, <i>Fade</i> wasn't my favorite book in the series. It felt less balanced than previous books, and there was a lot of telling rather than showing. This lead to some 'paraphrasing for the readers' sake' instances, and some events lacking build up or coming out of left field. Not typical for iCos. Another atypicality: some characters lacking depth or nuance (the new Marshall and Jordan as main examples).<br /><br />So yeah, was it perfect? No. Was it engaging? Hell yes! Will I miss this world, these characters? Oh yeah. <br /><br />Fade was a great ending to a superb series and journey, and I feel happy to have experienced it till the very end. <br />But I am so sad to say goodbye.<br /><br /> <br />A big shout out to Marleen and Kate, the super enablers. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11003533456562171251" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_588436692" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588436692" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4844873-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299680097p2/4844873.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588436692?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4844873-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4844873-laura?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588436692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6234577733121645571"><br/>***SPOILERS AHEAD***<br/><br/><b>”Lately it felt like every truth he ever thought he knew kept turning out to be a lie.”</b><br/><br/>What we want or need to believe and what’s true often get so twisted up and turned around. But Fade takes it to a whole new level. The intensity level is turned <i>way</i> up for the last installment of the In the Company of Shadows series. Despair, longing, action, humor, and suspense bring Fade to life in vivid pain and passion. The twists & turns, shocks, and connections will keep you on the ed</span>
  <span id="freeText6234577733121645571" style="display:none"><br />***SPOILERS AHEAD***<br /><br /><b>”Lately it felt like every truth he ever thought he knew kept turning out to be a lie.”</b><br /><br />What we want or need to believe and what’s true often get so twisted up and turned around. But Fade takes it to a whole new level. The intensity level is turned <i>way</i> up for the last installment of the In the Company of Shadows series. Despair, longing, action, humor, and suspense bring Fade to life in vivid pain and passion. The twists &amp; turns, shocks, and connections will keep you on the edge of your seat, jumping, muttering, and guessing until the end! So come on…let’s do this!<br /><br />This is the hardest review I’ve ever had to write. There is no way to express my love for this story without saying certain things. So please if you plan to read this series—turn back now. <br /><br />Fade pretty much kicked my ass! Pain, sobs, and heartache ripped my heart to shreds. Pain I could feel bone deep. Words and emotions that hit home, latched on, and curled around my heart and soul. I found it hard to breath at times, choking on my tears, trying so hard to keep them in as Boyd broke my heart. Wait! Scratch that. Tore my heart out with a spoon! The loss, grief, and pain were palpable on the page. Depression so thick at times I could feel it tugging me down.<br /><br /><b>”It was getting harder to breathe evenly and he recognized the deeply gouging sorrow that was ready to engulf him. That-too familiar pain and hopelessness that would surely become as equal a master of his life as the Agency was.”</b><br /><br />Beautiful, heart breaking words caught Boyd’s tears, longing, disbelief, shock, and desperation on the page. As he clung and curled up to his memories and ghosts of the past—all I wanted to do was hug him and never let go! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ It is amazing how Sin’s presence still held such power on the page in the first half of the book. Even though he wasn’t there, I could still feel and see him through Boyd’s pain and memories. Boyd kept Hsin alive on the page for me with the memories of his fingers running through his hair, the sound of his heartbeat in his ear, and whispered words I could hear as clear as day—“I don’t want you to go.” Sometimes I felt like Hsin was right there in the scene next to Boyd whispering the words again to him. Stunning moments of pain that gave me *shivers*  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Then….BOOM! The world came to a full stop. Wait. Let me breathe here…*inhale, exhale*. There were actually several moments in Fade that I felt like my heart and world skidded to a halt. Powerful gut punches of action and emotions that blew me away! Everything began to take shape and connect. The secrets, revelations, and conspiracy all came to a head with such shock and suspense I couldn’t click fast enough. <br /><br />The connections! Pieces began to snap into place. Emotions and experiences from way back in book one played a part here. Dejavues and echoes of past experiences ripped through the action bringing all four books together in one powerful punch! Drawings capturing a time in the first book helped jog memories here; journals helped unlock long ago secrets; kisses and blood kicked lust and hunger alive again; and LOVE held on and survived no matter how hard someone tried to wipe it all away. And I don’t mean these scenes or words just reminded me of other times—they fucking pulled me right back to those moments with force. I could feel it all over again! Pure brilliance! The writing and planning truly brought me to my knees in this book. I have never experienced such a powerful all-encompassing finale before. The whole series came full circle in so many ways. The power and impact of all four books hit me like a fucking brick wall. Hit me full force! It’s stunning really. As Boyd slid into a diner booth here in Fade, my head and heart couldn’t help but experience another late night diner experience filled with questions, flirting, and fun. I could feel the tension again—see those long fingers stir his sweet, thick shake. *sigh* <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ A father’s plea echoes off of his son’s from so long ago…”Please don’t hate me”. Both scenes came to life, overlapping, and impacting this story and my heart all over again. History and past pains haunted these pages creating one very powerful experience.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Anyway…I know I’m rambling. I could go on and on. But truth be told—I’m exhausted. This journey has been a privilege to experience, but damn I feel gutted at the moment. There is a hole in my gut right now that I can’t seem to fill. I can’t believe it’s over. I’m in shock. <br /><br />Thank you, Sonny and Ais. *bows head in awe*<br /><br /><br /><u>The Ending</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I have huge mixed feeling about the epilogue. For me, the offer to go back and run the Agency broke my heart. After fighting so hard to get out, I would hate to see them go back even if they were running the show. Go forward. Move on. Go kick some ass in Mexico City with Captain America and his adorable sidekick!  I will follow these guys anywhere though—who am I kidding! <br /><br />There was a lot to love about the ending as well though. There is hope for more…  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u> My Viv</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[BITCH to the end! Haha…I kinda love you for it too. You did show a pulse at the very end though. Thank you for at least giving Boyd an explanation. He deserved it.<br /><br />I can’t help but wonder why I can’t forgive you. I forgave Emilio for being a shitty ass parent—abandoning Sin for 20 years. Why can’t I forgive you though? You did protect Boyd at times, but….nope. Can’t do it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>Carhart</u><br /><br />Zach, Zach, Zach! You frustrated the hell out of me in this one! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[But I still love you. :)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Favorite line: <b>”Are you sure you aren’t a porn star?”</b> :D<br /><br /><br /><u>Ryan</u><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Oh, Ryan! Be safe little man. You kickass little “minx”!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br /><br /><br /><u>This is a TRUE spoiler. Do not click if you plan to read this series.</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Emilio! <br /><br />You stole my heart—you slut! :) It took a long time, but once you got under my skin, you ruled the show with passion, love, and a no-holds bar attitude. I love that you can’t hide how you feel. Broke my heart and pulled me in!<br /><br />Favorite Lines (You can’t pick just one.)<br /><br /><b>”How fuckin’ sweet. You know you is in a room full of agents when the dude offering to smack a ho is deemed the white knight.”</b> <br /><br /> LOL! Only E could get away with that comment. <br /><br />This was one of two big sob and snot moments in this book for me…<br /><br /><b>”And he was…he was my boy. Nobody ever believes me but I really…” A hesitation. “I…you know. You know what I mean.”</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br /><u>Boyd &amp; Hsin</u><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I don’t even know what to say here. Just find your peace and hold on to each other—love each other always! <br /><br />They both have way too many moments to list. <br /><br />Boyd’s running hug was my second sob moment btw….Broke me! After almost two years--it was his hug and words that made me completely break down on the train one night. <br /><br />Hsin….um…..I’m going to go with this line just because it fucking turned me on. :D<br /><br /><b>”So tell me what you know or I will rip your fucking jugular open with my teeth.”</b> hehe….What? It’s hot!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br />So that’s it. The end. <br /><br />Fingers crossed we get lots more from all of these characters someday. I miss the energy and camaraderie already. <br /><br />Thanks to the whole ICoS gang for holding my hand through this journey.<br /><br />I never would have made it alone. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9772458396125172914">Rating removed!<br/><br/><b>M.I.N.D.-B.L.O.W.I.N.G.</b><br/><br/><br/>This...<br/><br/><blockquote>

They disappeared into the shadows, walking away from the unceasing narration that droned during the program, and away from the journalists who had helped them to finish it all.<br/>Soon, their boots were crunching on the snow outside. Soon, breath ghosted out into the cold air, and Sin led Boyd away from the property.<br/><br/>Their hands clasped again, and this time neither let g</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9772458396125172914" style="display:none">Rating removed!<br><br><b>M.I.N.D.-B.L.O.W.I.N.G.</b><br><br><br>This...<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464464266ra/19242178.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><i>Boyd didn't protest when their fingers locked, and Sin tugged him out of the room. They disappeared into the shadows, walking away from the unceasing narration that droned during the program, and away from the journalists who had helped them to finish it all.<br>Soon, their boots were crunching on the snow outside. Soon, breath ghosted out into the cold air, and Sin led Boyd away from the property.<br><br>Their hands clasped again, and this time neither let go.</i><br><br><br>...is exactly what kept me from turning into a total wreck: the fact, that Sin and Boyd are finally together. For good.<br><br><br>Fade began with a stab right into the heart and from this moment on, it was an emotional ride I won't forget so easily. Not by a long shot.<br><br>The previous book ended with a sort of a cliffhanger, but the beginning of Fade didn't make it any easier. It didn't solve anything. In the contrary, a multitude of new obscurities came up.<br><br><b>Did this book make me laugh?</b><br><br>Yes. Surprisingly often. <br><br><i>“Did we ever have a threesome?”<br>Kassian nearly choked on the coffee he'd just swallowed, and spit it back into the cup. He coughed violently, wincing and set it down on the counter. After he was finished embarrassing himself thoroughly, he shot Sin an incredulous stare.<br>“I'm sorry, WHAT?”<br>“I told you I had strange dreams a lot, and most of them seem to be actual memories. So I was wondering if that one was.”<br>“You had a dream that we had a threesome?”<br>“Yeah. We were--” Sin stopped, and shook his head. “Well, you don't need to know the details.”<br>“Maybe I want to know them.”<br>“That's why you don't need to know them.” The look Sin shot Kassian wasn't exactly warning, but it was getting there. “I was asking, not inviting you to have one.”</i><br><br><br><b>Did this book make me want to scream and strangle certain characters because of their cold and cruel behavior?</b><br><br>Definitely yes.<br><br><i>Her eyebrows lowered, darkening her eyes. “All times when your termination could have, did, or should have come up... and was avoided, miraculously, as if some god shone on you. Do you know what that tells me?” She leaned forward and didn't wait for him to answer before she continued flatly, “It tells me you're a liability.”</i><br><br><br><b>Did this book make me cry?</b><br><br>Yes, yes and once again... yes. More often than I can count. <br><br><i>"Boyd. You should rest."<br>"I can't. I'll--" I'll lay down and I'll think of him. I'll close my eyes and dream of him. I'll convince myself he's still here. I'll wake up and every time, every time I'm alone and the bed is cold and I remember I'm all on my own now it'll rip me apart--</i><br><br><br>Sin and Boyd had to go through so much, it was impossible not to take part and feel their pain, their loss, their hopelessness and the urgent need to protect the one they love. <br><br><br><b>Do I want to leave their world?</b><br><br>No. Absolutely not! <br><br>There's twists and turns you never would have expected. One minute you'd think everything is fine and next thing you knew, the shit had already hit the fan. And even if the whole story culminated in a showdown which has no equal, there are still so many open questions, I desperately hope to find the answers to in the following anthology.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2212857908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8939445424180525687">God<i>damn</i> it with this series. It's managed to completely destroy me and reduce me to a barely functioning human being. I'm pretty sure everyone's mad at me for completely ignoring them these past few days. I couldn't put it down. I was up till 2 am reading it. Until my eyes were so tired that I couldn't read the next paragraph.<br/><br/>I can't believe it's finished! I'm in shock with everything that happened. I don't even know if I'm in the best state of mind to write a review. Everything is too fresh and</span>
  <span id="freeText8939445424180525687" style="display:none">God<i>damn</i> it with this series. It's managed to completely destroy me and reduce me to a barely functioning human being. I'm pretty sure everyone's mad at me for completely ignoring them these past few days. I couldn't put it down. I was up till 2 am reading it. Until my eyes were so tired that I couldn't read the next paragraph.<br /><br />I can't believe it's finished! I'm in shock with everything that happened. I don't even know if I'm in the best state of mind to write a review. Everything is too fresh and I just want to start weeping of sadness and happiness all at once. Though, I don't think I have more tears on me. This book left me dehydrated. <br /><br />I can't even think coherently right now. All I can say this was an amazing experience. A such well-written story that touched so many aspects that left me speechless. Kudos to the authors.<br /><br />It's addictive. As I said, I couldn't put it down. Many times I will wake up at 6 am to keep reading. Yes, that's the only way I can voluntarily wake up at those ungodly hours.<br /><br />I mean, how cannot I be obsessed if it's full of romance, soul-shattering moments, action, suspense, comedy, hotness and of course, "OMG, I CAN'T BELIEVE THAT HAPPENED","PLEASE DON'T LET HIM BE DEAD" or "Fucking die already, bitch!" screams? All those factors create a mind-blowing story, impossible not to want to devour it. <br /><br />I didn't know what to expect with Fade, but the whole series certainly ruined my life. I still can't shake the feeling of terror and heartache I had from the very beginning. <b>This book is +10000 stars for me</b> and I'd undergo all the pain of reading it again because it's totally worthy and who knows if I missed something the first time around? <br /><br />I'm completely in love with these books and with Boyd, Hsin, Emilio, Zach, Ryan, Kassian, Owen, Harriet, and so on... ;) <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I just can't believe Boyd lost his eye. My only comfort is to think that a pirate look might work perfectly on him. Still, as I told Vir: <i>Es mejor tuerto, que muerto.</i> ;P  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2911840791277843636"><b>5++ stars for the whole series</b> : the word « epic » is often used in the reviews, well it’s well earned.<br/><br/>When I jumped from “The Interludes” to “Fade”, I was wondering what was going to happen. Well, I didn’t have to wait for long : it started right away. <br/>And once again : the despair, the anguish, the longing, the questioning…oh my, and the hotness !!<br/>I’ve been binge-reading this last part because I just had to !!!<br/><br/>This series is fascinating, insane, addictive, painful, heartbreaking. But oh, so muc</span>
  <span id="freeText2911840791277843636" style="display:none"><b>5++ stars for the whole series</b> : the word « epic » is often used in the reviews, well it’s well earned.<br /><br />When I jumped from “The Interludes” to “Fade”, I was wondering what was going to happen. Well, I didn’t have to wait for long : it started right away. <br />And once again : the despair, the anguish, the longing, the questioning…oh my, and the hotness !!<br />I’ve been binge-reading this last part because I just had to !!!<br /><br />This series is fascinating, insane, addictive, painful, heartbreaking. But oh, so much worth it. Quite an unique experience. And the ending….a closure as well as an opening, because yes, how to let go of Hsin &amp; Boyd, and all the others, Ryan, Zach, Emilio, Kassian, Owen,….<br /><br />Thumbs up for the authors : 3.820 pages and yet, I still want more.<br /><br /><b>HIGHLY recommended !!</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16346028348957733907">5 +++ stars<br/><br/>Two cases of wine, 3 boxes of tissues, 4 ruined fingernails, 5 bars of chocolate, 20 days, about 32 breathless ‘I can't believe it’, multiple (usually horrified) Oh No!s, and uncountable, emotionally-laden OMGs later ….. I’m finished with the series. (Oh, and there may have been the odd Wtf on the way, too.)<br/><br/>And what a read it’s been! Incredible. Fabulous. Spectacular. Consuming. Heart-wrenching. Oh so heart-wrenching. Poignant. Touching. Agonizing. Excruciating. Overwhelming. Steamy a</span>
  <span id="freeText16346028348957733907" style="display:none">5 +++ stars<br><br>Two cases of wine, 3 boxes of tissues, 4 ruined fingernails, 5 bars of chocolate, 20 days, about 32 breathless ‘I can't believe it’, multiple (usually horrified) Oh No!s, and uncountable, emotionally-laden OMGs later ….. I’m finished with the series. (Oh, and there may have been the odd Wtf on the way, too.)<br><br>And what a read it’s been! Incredible. Fabulous. Spectacular. Consuming. Heart-wrenching. Oh so heart-wrenching. Poignant. Touching. Agonizing. Excruciating. Overwhelming. Steamy and sizzling HOT. So many fitting adjectives and yet, they can’t even begin to describe ICoS adequately.<br><br>‘Fade’ is the crowning glory in my opinion (and hence went straight on my ‘best-of-the-best shelf), and it's my favourite for a few reasons. <br><br>.) Starting with a bang, it was fast paced, giving me hardly enough time to breathe right up to the last chapter. With turns and twists at every corner it kept me on tenterhooks every single second.<br><br>( I did use the same pics for Evenfall, but wanted to include them here at the end...I know Boyd will look more mature and built, but still - to me that's the essence of them. :) )<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472752430i/20238129._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472752182i/20238103._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>.) Boyd and Sin – if you thought this couldn’t get better or more heart-rending – think again. What these two have to get through just to be together … is beyond comprehension. That’s why the end is one of the most gratifying things ever! I particularly loved when they got all domestic <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Boyd baking, Sin setting the table… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and we saw them in some kind of NORMAL situation.<br><br>.) Emilio – God, I love this man, and who could resist that smart-ass, cheeky, gorgeous bad boy? He certainly got some of the best lines in the book. <br><b> “It’s hard being this fucking pretty.” Emilio turned to the side eyeing his profile in the mirror.”<br>“You named your car’s computer <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ los mas chingan?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> </b><br><br>But what makes him ultimately attractive in my books is his inherent vulnerability. The way he can’t say that he loves someone. The way we know he is desperate for love and affection. The way he puts on the hard-ass- don’t care-mask when he’s dying inside. The way he is such a lonely and lost soul, I just want to….. sigh. You see what I mean.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474391710i/20593364._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>.) The expressiveness of the writing struck me particularly in this last book. E.g Boyd’s grief and desperation at the beginning was brilliantly observed and beautifully executed over two whole chapters! I was emotionally destroyed (in the best possible way) after it. That is what excellent authors do.<br><br>Needless to mention the intensity of the sex, the intricacy of the plot or the most brilliant secondary characters! Or the sheer addiction that comes with it. Just brace yourself.  Believe me – it might be tough, but I loved all of it! <br><br>One thing though – I was left with a few niggles (I will not discuss here and now) and quite a few questions, with one worry in particular. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Although I understand why Boyd and Sin decide to return at the end, it worries me. Because Matthew treats them just like they were treated before, he has no respect for them, so how is this plan of his going to work? Will the boys end up in a similar situation as before? Even if they take the position they are promised it might be hard for them to stick to their own standards.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>I’m more than grateful that ICoS was completed before I discovered it. Waiting for instalments would have killed me. And I do thank Sonny and Ais quietly for the 1/27 anthology that’s waiting for me once I’m done with this review….<br>A brilliant finish to an exceptional series!<br><br>HIGHLY RECOMMENDED</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16346028348957733907" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19818900-karen-wellsbury?shelf=put-aside-for-now">put-aside-for-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19818900-karen-wellsbury?shelf=just-putting-to-one-side">just-putting-to-one-side</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1049892976" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10866811000390953554">When I read the last page of Fade, I felt abandoned.<br/>I started reading ICoS on my holiday, and so for the last 5 months it's been part of my reading life, I have questioned some of the twists and turns of the plot, loved and hated various characters and constantly rooted for a properly happy ending..and now its finished ?<br/><br/>To use the word epic is an understatement, this is story telling on a massive scale, over 5000 pages, 5 (or 4 volumes depending on which version you read), excluding 1/27. But it</span>
  <span id="freeText10866811000390953554" style="display:none">When I read the last page of Fade, I felt abandoned.<br />I started reading ICoS on my holiday, and so for the last 5 months it's been part of my reading life, I have questioned some of the twists and turns of the plot, loved and hated various characters and constantly rooted for a properly happy ending..and now its finished ?<br /><br />To use the word epic is an understatement, this is story telling on a massive scale, over 5000 pages, 5 (or 4 volumes depending on which version you read), excluding 1/27. But it's so alive, I really cared for these characters in a way that I haven't with many other books. I can honestly say that it caused some major emotions as well, the beginning of this book, I went through the wringer, it was just so incredibly sad, then it lifted me up, then I was angry, then bemused, then sad... you get the picture. <br />Undercut all of this with the desire to find out who is good, who can be trusted, who has what agenda, and then there is the action... which is amazing, several times I did the reenactment thing, getting actual people to move and see does that really work? (pick young flexible people if you're tempted to try this out).<br /><br />So, it's an epic love story, it's edge of your seat exciting, it's a disturbing view of humankind's ability to completely mess everything up, it's hopeful and tender, one of the best things I have ever read and it's free(kudos and thanks to Santino and Ais )<br /><br /><br />If you've read it, then you know how good ICoS is, and if you haven't you should - really you should<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10866811000390953554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_545488554" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/545488554" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4713337-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434637089p2/4713337.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/545488554?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/4713337-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4713337-karen?shelf=mm-read">mm-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer545488554" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15726979531455802855">Where to begin? That's a hell of a question when pondering this series. From start to finish I was drawn in, compelled to keep reading even when I felt like taking a break and reading something else, even just a short story before continuing on. There was always a nagging voice in the back of my brain saying 'no' so I kept reading.<br/><br/>The scariest part of this series was the setting. Set in a world that is post World War III. We are presented with a future that holds very real possibilities, very be</span>
  <span id="freeText15726979531455802855" style="display:none">Where to begin? That's a hell of a question when pondering this series. From start to finish I was drawn in, compelled to keep reading even when I felt like taking a break and reading something else, even just a short story before continuing on. There was always a nagging voice in the back of my brain saying 'no' so I kept reading.<br /><br />The scariest part of this series was the setting. Set in a world that is post World War III. We are presented with a future that holds very real possibilities, very believable characters making choices that lead sometimes to unforeseen consequences.<br /><br />Were there flaws in this series sure there were just like in life there are always flaws and sometimes it's the flaws that add to the perfection. In The Company of Shadows was a free read and the sad part of that is I have read books that I paid good, hard earned money for that did not provide me with the hours and hours of entertainment that this story did. Did not leave me feeling like my visit with so many dear friends was at an end, hopefully just for now (I still have the side &amp; back stories to enjoy at the very least).<br /><br />Fade was the culmination of the war between the agency &amp; Janus, but it was also the resolution to so many other secondary storylines that were woven throughout. <br /><br />The list of characters that I became attached to was probably the longest list of any series I have ever read. Of course Sin &amp; Boyd top that list. The hell that they both endured especially Boyd. I found myself alternately ranting and sobbing endlessly over what they suffered both separately and together. Ryan is without a doubt the techno geek of my heart, I want to keep him. He is one of the most adorable and loveable characters I have ever encountered. Carhart and Emilio, while this pairing was not a surprise the way the dynamics between these two developed was incredibly well done. The strength and intensity of their relationship was so reflective of the strength and intensity of character they each possessed. Kassian broke my heart, he was broken &amp; damaged and fought so hard to try and fix himself but I don't think he quite knew how. He is definitely a work in progress. To varying degrees there were other characters that I enjoyed but this was the core group who garnered my affection and stole my attention without fail.<br /><br />I've left Vivienne for the end. Why you might wonder? Because I liked her that much? Oh hell no! I hated Vivienne, wanted her destroyed. As a mother and a person she failed epically. But at the end when events were unfolding the authors presented her in a way that made me think, made me wonder. It was like dominoes if her childhood had been different, if her husband had lived, if she'd known certain things sooner, would she have behaved the way she did, would she have been a different person...a better person? These things remained unanswered and I like that, it leaves it for the reader to decide. <br /><br />I gave Fade 5 stars because there weren't more than that to be given and while the previous books in this series were 5 star reads for me Fade was more so much more. I was left with a sense of completion to the story but at the same time I was left with things to consider to think about. My brain and my heart were engaged from start to finish and beyond. In my eyes that is the sign of an author's job being very well done and I can want nothing more.<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15726979531455802855" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15247690225126047270">Boyd comes back from his long valentine mission. But something is amiss. Something big. Something important. He must find a way to live without him, but he doesn't think he needs to...   <span id="freeText15247690225126047270" style="display:none">Boyd comes back from his long valentine mission. But something is amiss. Something big. Something important. He must find a way to live without him, but he doesn't think he needs to... He still has hope.<br /><br />An absolute work of art.<br />The depth to the characters, even the ones who don't have a big role is tremendous, I feel like I know all the characters in and out. There is a lot of heartbreak in this novel, so heed my forewarning, and fortify your heart! <br /><br />Fade has to be the best book in the series, the pace is even faster than the others, and so goddamn entertaining! It's a real page-turner. <br /><br />I enjoyed reading a little about Adam and Gordon, as I read about them in After Midnight, and was hoping to catch up on them. Hopefully more will be released...<br /><br /> <blockquote>
  <i>-The End of In the Company of Shadows-</i>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487568939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16186685876879977266">What an ending! It was every bit as climatic as it should have been for a series of this length. Fade grabs you from the first page and doesn't let go until you've choked up every last tear. It's impossible to really get into specifics without spoiling, but suffice it to say, if you've come this far you will not be disappointed. <br/><br/>ETA: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[It's been a few days and I'm still thinking about Boyd losing his goddamn eyeball. I don't think I've ever come across two characters getting shit on</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16186685876879977266" style="display:none">What an ending! It was every bit as climatic as it should have been for a series of this length. Fade grabs you from the first page and doesn't let go until you've choked up every last tear. It's impossible to really get into specifics without spoiling, but suffice it to say, if you've come this far you will not be disappointed. <br /><br />ETA: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It's been a few days and I'm still thinking about Boyd losing his goddamn eyeball. I don't think I've ever come across two characters getting shit on quite as much as these two. I've had to remind myself that it totally worked for Christian Slater in True Romance. Eyepatches can be kinda hot I guess. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_936780035" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/936780035" />
    <a title="Elsbeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14879044-elsbeth"><img alt="Elsbeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353801922p2/14879044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/936780035?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elsbeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elsbeth" href="/user/show/14879044-elsbeth">Elsbeth</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=m-m-romance-fiction">m-m-romance-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=sci-fi-dystopia-or-post-apocalyptic">sci-fi-dystopia-or-post-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=top-10-2014">top-10-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=worth-rereading">worth-rereading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=favorites-m-m">favorites-m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14879044-elsbeth?shelf=ruined-cause-of-behavior-author">ruined-cause-of-behavior-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer936780035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6733739414418924270"><br/><b>*rating removed</b><br/><br/>In order to support the victims of the despicable behavior of Santino, I will remove the rating but my review stands cause I just can't...... I'm so mad that my beloved Sin & Boyd are now ruined by Santino.<br/><br/>**********************************************<br/><br/><br/>I can't believe this is the end. I can't believe this journey is over. But there it was, written in black :<i>'The End of In the Company of Shadows'</i>. <br/><br/>This book had me crying, pulling my hair out from frustration, having severe heart att</span>
  <span id="freeText6733739414418924270" style="display:none"><br><b>*rating removed</b><br><br>In order to support the victims of the despicable behavior of Santino, I will remove the rating but my review stands cause I just can't...... I'm so mad that my beloved Sin &amp; Boyd are now ruined by Santino.<br><br>**********************************************<br><br><br>I can't believe this is the end. I can't believe this journey is over. But there it was, written in black :<i>'The End of In the Company of Shadows'</i>. <br><br>This book had me crying, pulling my hair out from frustration, having severe heart attack-moments, laughing out loud and rooting for these characters…. Pretty much all kinds of emotions you can think of, I have experienced in this series. Incredible!!!<br><br>I had a really hard time reading the first 30% of “Fade” because of the struggle Boyd was going through!! And although Sin was not with us this part, Boyd kept him alive for us in his mind. It was just heartbreaking… Also to learn what Boyd had endured during his last mission as valentine. This agency… I hated them. Boyd was so strong, how he dealt with everything. <br><br>My favorite part was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the homecoming of Boyd..  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Cried so much!!!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>"I love you, Hsin,"</b> he said hoarsely.<b>"I missed you so much."</b><br><b>"I love you, too."</b> Sin's voice was still thick and husky. <b>"I came back for you. Because I wanted to find you, because I wanted to remember you."</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I also liked Emilio and Zach together. Them caring so much for each other and for Boyd and Sin.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The last scene with Zach at the compound…. Crying again. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There were so much twists and turns in this book, my head kept spinning.<br><br>The end of the book was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[open <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and I am soooo hoping for book 5 The series can easily go on for another 1000 pages!!<br><br>But for now it’s time to say goodbye to;<br><br><b>Hsin “Sin”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384230147i/6820832._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>You stole my heart….<br><br><b>Boyd</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408991029i/10918431._SY540_.png" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>You came a long way to the grown man in book 4 who had to make all kind of difficult decisions…<br><br><b>Emilio</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379771858i/302335.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You had me laughing all the time!! You are so crazy…<br><br><b>Zach “Carhart”</b><br>You stood up for everyone….<br><br><b>Ryan</b><br>I love you man….<br><br><b>Kassian, Owen,</b> great characters!!<br><br><b>Vivienne,</b> uugghhhh<br><br>Goodbye my friends!!!<br><br>I’m feeling depressed now!! And one final warning:<b> DO NOT READ THIS SERIES UNLESS YOU ARE READY TO BE CONSUMED!!! BECAUSE IT WILL CONSUME EVERY THOUGHT YOU HAVE!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379788331i/508003.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8164566.Evenfall__In_the_Company_of_Shadows___1_" title="Evenfall (In the Company of Shadows, #1) by Santino Hassell" rel="nofollow noopener">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EROZ9O81UVgp1jG7o+97Dvbz5eXcXqa/6r020EIypNBYKWpTzvxu+LFiFJFjOw8n0YyKwD6X7ApTazsyRjikKg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ESJFI+chNRlXROEXXoVJqiH+SLdGpdqgwKYo2UVawBRYGLaExugKuc/wxD2eUT2DBoEnkqRskBV5cCU7QVDA7g==')})
  }
//]]>
